      module: "Global",
      action: "onClick",
      points: 0,
      timestamp: new Date(),

      attributes: {
        url: window.location.href,
        PartnerName: 'Button',
        CTAName: e.target.innerText,
        OfferName: document.title
      }
    });
  }
</script>

<h2 class="text-left">North and South America</h2>



<div class="richtext">









<p>Soak up the big city vibe in the USA. Perhaps delve into the east coast's New York or over to west coast to tech hub San Francisco. Those into the outdoors might choose to ski awesome mountains or kayak in the picturesque lakes of Canada.</p> 
<p>Home to the stunning Andes, the Amazonian rainforest and the dramatic Inca ruins, South America is a colourful paradise.</p></div>

</div>

<script>
  function handleArticleClick(e){
    e = e || window.event;
    window?.dataLayer?.setEvent({
      name: 'Article',
      module: "Global",
      action: "onClick",
      points: 0,
      timestamp: new Date(),
      categories: ['Article Global', "Qantas", "Loyalty"],
      attributes: {
        url: window.location.href,
        PartnerName: e.currentTarget.articleTitle,
        CTAName: e.target.innerText,
        OfferName: document.title
      }
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',(event)=>{
    const articleElements = document.getElementsByClassName("article   ");
    for (let j = 0; j< articleElements.length; j++){
      let linkElements = articleElements[j].getElementsByTagName('a');
      let headElements = articleElements[j].getElementsByTagName('h3');
      let heading = headElements.length > 0 ? headElements[0].textContent : 'Article';
      for(let i = 0; i< linkElements.length; i++){
        linkElements[i].addEventListener('click',handleArticleClick,false);
        linkElements[i].articleTitle = heading;
      }
    }
  },false);
</script>

<div class="article   ">
